A reconstruction may be a consolidation (reduction in the number of shares on issue) or a share split (increase in the number of shares on issue). So for example if there is a 3:1 consolidation then the number of shares are divided by three i.e. there is now one share for every three (previous) shares. A reconstruction may be a consolidation (reduction in the number of shares on issue) or a share split (increase in the number of shares on issue).
